Another thousand people broke through the security cordon and went to the Seiyukai headquarters at the first venue, joining the crowd there and engaging in a major clash with the police. Stones and bottles rained down, causing numerous injuries, and sixty-seven people were arrested.

Major Loss to Italian Aviation

Three Famous Aviators Perish Together

Reuters, Pissa, 19th: Three famous Italian aviators who recently participated in the Italian-South American flight, namely Army Colonel Maddalena, Army Captain Cocconi, and Engineering Lieutenant Damonte, perished together today. The cause of the accident is unknown, but people on the beach reported seeing the aircraft flown by the three suddenly plummeting into the sea from a height of about 1,500 feet.

National, Rome, 20th: This morning, all Italian newspapers displayed black borders to mourn the tragic death of the three famous aviators. Authorities searched the accident site overnight, recovering only two jackets and scattered items. The remains of the three have not yet been found. Italian Premier Mussolini telegraphed the Minister of Aviation, expressing deep sorrow and stating that Colonel Maddalena was the most daring and experienced member of the Italian Air Force.

Plot to Sabotage US Dirigible Discovered

Secret Agents Uncover Conspiracy

Hungarian Officer Arrested and Imprisoned

Dentsu, Akron, 20th: US secret agents discovered a plot to sabotage the Navy's under-construction airship Akron. The plotter, a former Hungarian Army officer named Gase, has been arrested and imprisoned. According to the Intelligence Department, Gase worked as a technician at the Goodyear Zeppelin factory in Akron. During his employment, he deliberately constructed the Akron's engine parts improperly and intentionally omitted several rivets from important parts, making it easier for the control car, which is central to the ship, to break. If this plot had succeeded, the airship would have crashed and been destroyed during its first test flight after completion.

Phoenix Lost En Route to the Philippines

Associated Press, Manila, 20th: Pilot White of American Airlines departed from Macau yesterday morning aboard the Phoenix en route to the Philippines. Its whereabouts are unknown. At dawn today, the US Navy dispatched four destroyers, an aircraft carrier, and the Army dispatched two aircraft to search everywhere. The Portuguese Army in Macau also dispatched a seaplane to search along the route towards Dongsha Island, but as of 10:30 AM, the aircraft has not been found.

Gandhi and Manufacturers Agree on Handling Foreign Cloth Issue

Reuters, Bombay, 19th: Gandhi discussed the issue of handling stockpiled foreign cloth with local manufacturers. They have now agreed to organize a company to purchase the existing foreign cloth in India and resell it abroad. The company will bear a portion of the losses. At the same time, the company will seek to encourage the production, sale, and distribution of self-woven cotton cloth throughout India.

Former German Chancellor's Condition Critical

Reuters, Berlin, 19th: Former Chancellor Dr. Muller is in critical condition. He is now unconscious and gradually weakening. He received a blood transfusion from doctors today.

Important News

Fifteenth Meeting of the National Government

Deadline Set for Compiling General Reports from Ministries and Departments

Northwest Academic Expedition Organized

Accounting Office to be Established on April 1st

The fifteenth meeting of the National Government was held on the morning of the 20th, attended by Yu Youren, Wang Chonghui, Song Ziwen, Shao Yuanchong, Dai Chuanxian, Chiang Kai-shek, and Sun Ke. Chiang Kai-shek chaired the meeting.

(A) Reports

(1) The Executive Yuan reported that the agreement to recover the Belgian concession in Tianjin, signed in August of the eighteenth year of the Republic, had been previously approved by the government. The Executive Yuan and representatives of the Belgian Embassy agreed to exchange ratification documents of the two governments in Beijing on the afternoon of the 18th. A copy of the full text of the agreement was submitted to the government for record and publication to complete the procedure.

(2) The Executive Yuan reported the regulations for commercial commissioners stationed abroad, passed by the State Council. In addition to being filed by the Yuan, the regulations were instructed to be published by the Ministry of Industry.

(3) The Executive Yuan's State Council decided on the appointment and dismissal of officials above the rank of Simplified Appointment:

(A) Luo Jialun's resignation as President of National Tsinghua University was approved, and Wu Nanxuan was appointed to fill the vacancy.

(B) Yuan Qifu's resignation as member and Director of Finance of the Qinghai Provincial Government was approved, and Wei Fuzhi was appointed to fill the concurrent vacancies.

(C) Cui Tingxian's long absence from duty as Mayor of Tianjin was terminated, and Zhang Xueming was appointed to fill the vacancy.

(D) Yao Xijiu was appointed as Counselor of the Ministry of Military Administration.

(E) Nie Kaiyi was promoted to Senior Technician of the Ministry of Communications and Zhuang Huan, Director of the Department of Telegraph Administration of the Ministry of Communications, was transferred to Counselor of the Ministry, and Zhong E was appointed as Director of the Department of Telegraph Administration.

(B) Discussion Items

(1) The Chairman proposed that a general report be submitted to the National Assembly on the progress of the affairs under the jurisdiction of each Yuan, Ministry, and Council since its establishment, as well as a comprehensive plan for the various important policies to be promoted and reformed. It was proposed that each Yuan be instructed to assign the Secretary-General of the Yuan to be responsible for compiling and submitting the report to the Civil Service Department by April 10 for compilation. A resolution was passed to proceed.

(2) The Chairman proposed that the government order various academic institutions to select experts and provide travel expenses to organize a Northwest Academic Expedition, stipulating a route to conduct on-site research on the geography, geology, biology, antiquities, and ethnology of the Northwest, limiting the period to four years and requiring the submission of a plan and outline with substantial results. A resolution was passed with revisions and first submitted to Commissioners Dai and Cai.

(3) The Executive Yuan and the Examination Yuan jointly reported that as China is in the initial stage of construction, various administrative and examination systems should broadly adopt foreign practices for reference. It was proposed to jointly send personnel to Japan for observation and to organize a preparatory committee to first study the scope of investigation by the members to ensure that it is adapted to China's needs. The Executive Yuan planned to select two members, and the Ministries of Education, Interior, and Industry would each send one member. The Examination Yuan planned to select two members, and the Examination Committee and the Department of Personnel would each send one member, totaling nine members. It was also proposed to depart in early April for a period of forty days. The estimated cost, based on maximum frugality, would be 31,525.20 yuan. It was requested that the Ministry of Finance be instructed to promptly allocate the full amount to facilitate the trip. A resolution was passed to proceed.

(4) A resolution was passed to promulgate the Special Examination Law.

(5) A resolution was passed to promulgate the Organizational Regulations of the Capital Rehabilitation Institute.

(6) A resolution was passed to promulgate the revised Provincial Government Organization Law.

(7) A resolution was passed to promulgate the Provisional Organizational Outline of the Sichuan Post-War Rehabilitation Commissioner's Office.

(8) A resolution was passed to formally establish the Accounting Office on April 1 of this year, appointing Chen Qicai as Director of Accounting and Liu Dajun, Pan Xulun, Qin Fen, Yang Shu, Mei Wu, and Wu Dajun as Accounting Officers, and appointing Chen Qicai concurrently as Director of the Budget Bureau.

(9) A resolution was passed to appoint Li Yuanding as Deputy Director of the Audit Department, Wang Wenhai as Secretary-General of the Audit Department, and Wang Peiyuan, Chang Longgui, Lin Jin, Yu Zhangcheng, Wen Yiyou, Liu Wenhai, and Zhou Zengkui as Auditors of the Audit Department.

(10) A resolution was passed to dismiss Chen Yifan, Secretary-General of the Construction Committee, and Xiao Wenxi, Nie Qiying, Qin Yu, Bao Guobao, Chen Maojie, Zhang Zili, and Yun Zhen, all councilors, director, and technican respectively, from their posts and to appoint Chen Yifan as Secretary-General, Liu Shixin and Zhang Jianxuan as Secretaries, Xiao Wenxi and Nie Qiying as Councilors, Qin Yu as Director of the General Affairs Office, Huo Baoshu as Director of the Design Office, and Zhang Zili, Yun Zhen, Zhu Yaoting, and Yu Jichuan as Technicians.

(11) The Executive Yuan reported that the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission had reported that the Xilhetu Kulun Banner had voluntarily requested the separation of politics and religion, and submitted five measures for the separation. The 16th meeting of the Yuan's State Council resolved to approve the original proposed measures for record, and requested prompt approval to appoint Luobuxang Linqin as Zasak of the Xilhetu Kulun Banner and to instruct the bureau to cast and issue seals. A resolution was passed to proceed.

(12) The Executive Yuan reported that the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission had reported that the late leader of the Zhuosotu League, Gongsang Nuorbu, had assisted in the Republic, maintained Mongolia and Tibet, and made meritorious contributions. It was requested that the government issue a clear order for preferential treatment and burial, and that the commission inform the local government officials along the route when the coffin of the late leader is returned to the banner from Beiping to provide proper care, and instruct the Rehe Provincial Government to prepare separate sacrifices to show extraordinary honors. A resolution was passed to proceed.

Remnants of Pinghan Railway Bandits Fleeing Eastward

Xu Yuanquan Supervises Suppression of Communist Bandits in Western Hubei

Hankou Correspondent: Since the Bian and Han Headquarters dispatched troops to encircle and suppress the bandits along the Pinghan Railway, the situation has stabilized in recent days, and the damaged bridges and roads are gradually being repaired. Commander-in-Chief Chiang, in order to ensure the permanent safety of the railway, specifically ordered the Kaifeng and Wuhan Headquarters to divide and guard the railway, and dispatched four artillery trains to patrol between Guangshui and Zhumadian to ensure thoroughness. The task of searching and suppressing the remnants of the bandits is the responsibility of Li Mingzhong, the Pacification Director of the Henan, Anhui, and Hubei border areas. The Wuhan Headquarters has transferred the First Aviation Team stationed in Hankou to dispatch several fighter planes daily to conduct reconnaissance to the north. If Communist bandits are discovered, they will be bombed at any time. After receiving the orders, the Bian and Han Headquarters made separate arrangements. Liu Zhi, Director of the Bian Headquarters, arrived in Xinyang on the 15th and returned to Bian on the 16th. Before leaving, he ordered Zhao Guantao and Yuan Ying to maintain close contact. Yesterday (the 18th), he also appointed Zhang Fang as the Commander-in-Chief for suppressing bandits in Southern Henan. All units of the 20th Route Army and the units of Zhao Guantao and Wan Dianzun are under his command and will depart immediately to supervise the suppression. He Chengjun, Director of the Wuhan Headquarters, ordered the troops stationed in the southern section of Wusheng Pass to thoroughly defend the area, and assigned Xiao Zhichu and Luo Zhuoying to carry out the search and suppression. He also ordered He Jingwu, Director of the Pinghan Railway Bureau, to expedite the repair of the tracks and bridges so that traffic can be restored as soon as possible. It is reported that the Communist bandits, due to the concentration of large forces in the southern section of the Pinghan Railway, fear being surrounded and have turned eastward. The leader of the bandits is unknown, but it is heard that Kuang Jixun is among them, perhaps the main force of the bandits. Director Li Mingzhong has taken a plane to Beijing to ask Chairman Chiang for instructions on everything. After returning to Hankou, he will depart to the east of Hubei to supervise Ji Hongchang and other units to encircle and suppress the bandits. In the western Hubei area, after Xu Yuanquan took office as the Director for Suppressing Bandits and Clearing Villages, he divided and dispatched troops to thoroughly suppress the bandits, and divided the responsibility for various areas with the Sichuan Army, Guo Xun, the Hunan Army, Li Jue, and the Guizhou Army, Luo Qijiang. Review of the 45th Division Stationed in Bengbu

Bengbu Correspondent: The Central Government, in order to reorganize the military and government and assess the strength of each division and brigade, has specially dispatched Chief of Staff Zhu Peide to inspect the troops stationed along the Tianjin-Pukou and Longhai Railways. Wu Qingzhi, the director of the first inspection team, Fan Yuying, the director of the second inspection team, and the inspection commissioners arrived in Bengbu at 3:30 PM on the morning of the 18th, crossing the Yangtze River from Nanjing by the second-class train on the Tianjin-Pukou Railway. Wu Qingzhi, along with the members of the first inspection team, Jin Jifang, Shen Zheng, Zhang Yazhun, Liu Fu, Zhang Pengwan, Zhang Zaiqin, and their attendants and escorts, disembarked and stayed at the Transportation Villa on Er Ma Road. Fan Yuying and others did not disembark and went to Xuzhou to inspect the 7th Division. Wei Lihuang, commander of the 45th Division here, had already received orders from the headquarters and concentrated his troops in Bengbu ten days ago to actively prepare. Director Wu informed the division headquarters last night of the schedule for inspecting the division. On the first day (the 19th), from 8:00 AM to 10:00 AM, the division's troops stationed in Bengbu will assemble at the airfield for a military parade. From 10:00 AM to 12:00 PM, there will be a review of field exercises. From 1:30 PM to 6:00 PM in the afternoon, there will be an inspection of personnel, horses, firearms, ammunition, and equipment at the airfield. On the second day (the 20th), from 8:00 AM to 12:00 PM, there will be a review of the 2nd Battalion of the 266th Regiment and the 2nd Regiment of the Independent Brigade, with field exercises for the engineering battalion and the communications company to set up telephones near Bengbu City. From 8:00 AM to 10:00 AM, there will be a review of the bayonet drill of the 1st Battalion of the 267th Regiment. From 10:00 AM to 12:00 PM, there will be a review of the earthwork operations of the 3rd Battalion of the 265th Regiment at the airfield. From 1:30 PM to 3:30 PM in the afternoon, there will be a review of the academic subjects of the 1st Battalion of the 268th Regiment, with soldiers at the West Third Barracks and officers in the training class lecture hall. At the same time, there will be live-fire shooting practice for the 267th Regiment at Lao Chu Mountain (two members will be assigned from each company to participate). On the third day (the 21st), from 8:00 AM to 12:00 PM and from 1:30 PM to 6:00 PM in the afternoon, there will be a review of the division, brigade, regiment, battalion, and company headquarters, barracks, warehouses, and hospitals, inspecting the internal affairs and checking the uniforms, equipment, instruments, vehicles, and equipment. The independent 1st Regiment stationed in Hao County and the 270th Regiment in Woyang will be separately inspected by members dispatched by Director Wu. As soon as the First Inspection Team has completed the review of the 45th Division, it will go to Kaifeng to review the 1st Division of Hu Zongnan, the Cavalry Brigade of Zhang Qiaoling, and the Independent Artillery Regiment, and then to Luoyang to review the 9th Division of Chiang Tingwen and to Huayin to review the 3rd Division of Chen Jicheng. The two teams are expected to complete the review by the end of April. Chief of Staff Zhu Peide arrived in Bengbu at 7:30 AM this morning (the 19th) by special train from Pukou at 1:00 AM. Military and police officials here welcomed him at the station. After Zhu disembarked, he was accompanied by Wei Lihuang to the Tang Garden Division Headquarters for a meal. At about 8:00 AM, he went to the Xiaoshan South Airfield for a military parade. The 45th Division dispatched troops to distribute posts along the way with strict security. (March 19)

The Termination of the Taiyuan Headquarters

Establishment of a Termination Office to Handle the Closure. Li Fuying to Leave for Shenyang Within Days to Urge the Allocation of Funds. Taiyuan Correspondence: After the cancellation of the Jin-Sui Garrison Headquarters, it was proposed to establish a Jin-Sui Military Termination Office to handle the closing affairs of the headquarters. However, this matter is of great importance and must be approved by the Northeast before it can be started. The army commanders had sent a telegram to Deputy Commander Zhang with the agreed results and the proposed plan for instructions. They received a reply expressing agreement. Therefore, Xu Shang, Yang, and others decided at a headquarters meeting on the 13th to officially establish the Jin-Sui Military Termination Office on the 15th of this month. The original eight departments of the headquarters were reduced to eight groups: Chief of Staff Group Lian Zhuangqiu, Chief of Military Affairs Group Fu Penghai, Chief of Military Supplies Group Guo Dianping, Chief of Ordnance Group Zhou Weihan, Chief of Military Medicine Group Bo Guitang, Chief of Military Law Group Lang Fenggeng, Chief of General Affairs Group Gao Guancheng, and Chief of Telecommunications Group Zhai Xiushan. After deducting the monthly expenditure of 80,000 for councilors, the original budget for the eight departments of the headquarters was approximately 30,000. This would be reduced by two-thirds, resulting in a monthly expenditure of slightly over 10,000. However, it is said that the chiefs of the Military Supplies and Military Affairs groups are unwilling to take office. The position of director has been decided as Shi Rongxi. The affairs handled by this office are limited to all matters that should be terminated, and they will not be involved in matters concerning various troops or military institutions. Furthermore, as this office is of a short-term nature, no new seal will be made, and the old seal of the Jin-Sui Garrison Commander will continue to be used for official documents. It is reported that the pre-scheduled time limit is three months, during which all termination matters will be completed and then the office will be abolished. If it cannot be completed by then, it may be extended for one or two months before being canceled again. Regarding the issue of funding allocation, Shang Xu, Yang, and Li Fuying, along with Fu Zhan魁, Men Zhizhong, and others, had a long discussion at the Shanxi Grand Hotel on the evening of the 14th. It was decided to send Li Fuying to Shenyang to meet with Zhang in person to present the actual difficulties of the Jin faction's military pay situation and urge the allocation of funds. Currently, the Jin faction's military pay has only been paid up to November of last year, with arrears reaching four months. A large sum of money is urgently needed to facilitate demobilization. According to Li Fuying, the generals have completed the inspection of their respective units and recommended him to go to Shenyang to request demobilization funds from Zhang. He decided to leave Taiyuan within three days. He also stated that the inspection of the troops stationed in northern Shanxi by Ji Yiqiao had yielded excellent results. Ji expressed that Deputy Commander Zhang would, of course, be responsible for the issue of military pay after this inspection and demobilization, and asked all generals, officers, and soldiers to rest assured.

Yesterday, Deputy Commanders Xu and Yang sent a telegram to all units, ordering them to quickly prepare rosters of demobilized officers and soldiers and report the total amount of arrears in pay in order to expedite the allocation of funds. The telegram stated: It has been found that the arrears in pay for December of last year and January and February of this year for various departments and battalions had previously been ordered to be allocated by the Bureau of Provisions. However, due to insufficient funds, it has not been possible to allocate the full amount in a timely manner. However, the demobilization of troops has been completed, and it is inappropriate for demobilized officers and soldiers to remain for long waiting for pay. The following measures are now stipulated: (1) The total amount of arrears in pay for each month for the demobilized officers and soldiers of each unit should be telegraphed immediately in order to instruct the bureau to expedite the allocation. (2) The arrears in pay for the remaining officers and soldiers retained will be collected after the first item has been completed. In addition to sending separate telegrams, it is hoped that you will investigate and handle this accordingly without delay, as this is extremely important. (March 16)

Shandong Businessmen's Federation Petition Regarding Business Tax

Jinan Correspondence: The Shandong Provincial Businessmen's Federation specially convened a meeting in Jinan for the implementation of the business tax by the provincial government. Yesterday (the 17th), the chairman of the Businessmen's Federation, Xin Zhujiu, representative of the Yantai Chamber of Commerce, Lin Songpu, chairman of the Zhoucun Chamber of Commerce, Li Huafeng, representative of the Linqing Chamber of Commerce, Lu Jiting, representative of the Yidu Chamber of Commerce, Ma Fangchuan, representative of the Heze Chamber of Commerce, Ma Shiyin, representative of the Boshan Chamber of Commerce, Xiahou Hongru, representative of the Ziyang Chamber of Commerce, Zhu Xinqing, went to the Finance Department to meet with Director Wang Xiangrong and deliver a petition regarding the collection of business tax, putting forward three requirements: (1) The total tax should be paid once a year, with shops divided into levels but goods not divided into levels. (2) If goods must be divided into levels, please reduce the categories (such as the business tax rate proposed by Shandong, where goods are divided into five categories for taxation, please reduce it to three or two categories). (3) The collection procedure should be simple, and it is best for the county governments or finance bureaus to collect and remit to the provincial treasury without setting up separate bureaus to avoid harassment. Wang Xiangrong expressed that the three requirements were difficult to implement and could not be approved. The representatives of the Businessmen's Federation also requested: (1) Those who pay consolidated tax should not pay business tax again. (2) Handicrafts such as straw hats and braids should be taxed lightly and not listed as luxury goods. (3) The collection procedure should be as simple as possible. Wang expressed that the latter three requirements could be discussed and said that the implementation of the business tax was just beginning, and it was difficult to estimate how much could be collected. It was estimated that the annual amount would be about 5 million yuan. The government sympathized with the difficulties of businesses and would not cause any harassment. The Businessmen's Federation has now closed its meeting and has appointed the petition representatives to be stationed in Jinan to study the business tax issue. The petition is recorded as follows: It has been found that the implementation of hidden levies and the implementation of business tax to make up for the accumulated malpractices of a hundred years. Once exempted, it is indeed pleasing to businessmen. I would like to offer the Director my humble opinions: (1) Handicrafts should be taxed lightly. My country's handicrafts are the source of livelihood for the poor. For example, hairnets, lace, and embroidery are all handicrafts. They are luxury goods domestically, but trade with foreign countries requires encouragement of exports, and customs duties have always been exempted. Therefore, the business tax rate should be determined lightly. (2) The collection procedure should be simple. The disadvantage of the former Likin was that there were numerous bureaus and cards, and the procedures were cumbersome, which was inconvenient for businessmen. The collection of business tax should be corrected. It is best to set up as few bureaus as possible and to be lenient in inspection. Harassment is worse than heavy taxes. For example, in matters such as checking accounts, the types of goods in a store often differ, and the tax rates are different. If it is necessary to classify and carefully seek it, it will inevitably be impossible to cope with and the burden will be unbearable. Therefore, the tax audit should be based on the main points and not be harsh, so as to prevent abuses and conform to the business situation. (3) Goods that have already been collected with special tax should be exempted. If special tax is levied again, it is double taxation. For example, coal in Boshan is a necessary commodity, and wine in Yantai can resist foreign wine. All have special taxes and should not be taxed again, depriving people of their needs and benefiting the infusion of foreign wine. I have stated above whether it is appropriate to ask your hearing to review and adopt it. It is for the public convenience.

The Eighteenth Annual Financial Report of the Ministry of Finance (Continued 4)

Silver Price Problem The gold and silver parity has fallen by half in the past two years, and the dismal fall in 1929 was even worse. Even today, the price of silver is still sluggish. As a result, the government, merchants, and consumers of foreign goods are all greatly affected. Fortunately, not many of our citizens use foreign goods, so although the international silver price has plummeted, the purchasing power of domestic silver coins has not fallen too low. However, in the event of crop failure, the problem of food supply must be solved by purchasing food from gold-using countries, and the situation will be dire. At the same time, once this widespread economic decline gradually improves, the low price of silver will instead increase the export of domestic products. This is also a fact that cannot be ignored. Silver prices have fallen so much, and the world economic situation is so depressed, but the production of silver has not decreased significantly. This is because silver is a by-product of refining other metals. In addition, the fineness of silver coins in Western countries has been reduced, and India has also adopted the gold standard and sold the remaining silver to the world silver market. Although the amount of sales is huge, there is still a lot of surplus silver. Moreover, due to the economic downturn in various countries, the demand for Chinese exports has also been sharply reduced. Looking at 1929, there was a period when our country actually had surplus silver exports, which shows the situation.

Regarding the silver price problem, the government has repeatedly consulted with the governments of various countries last year, intending to solve this problem through international cooperation, and is willing to do its best to promote it. However, to date, there is still no practical plan for international cooperation. If various countries have practical measures to rectify the silver price, our government will assist in its implementation at any time. Now that the silver price has fallen so badly, the need for our country to improve its monetary system is becoming increasingly obvious. The government is paying attention to this matter as a major problem at present.

Budget The government's budget deficit is an urgent problem. In the 17th year (ending June 1928), the treasury deficit reached 80 million yuan, and the capital of 20 million yuan borrowed for the establishment of the Central Bank was not included. In the 18th year (ending June 1929), the deficit was 101 million yuan. In the first half of the 19th year (ending December 1929), the deficit was even greater due to high military spending. The amount of borrowing alone reached 96 million yuan. Although the new taxes to offset the abolition of Likin in the second half of the 19th year (January to June 1931) have not been fully implemented, the treasury burden is heavy, and the deficit can be reduced later. If there are no unexpected accidents, it may be possible to achieve a balance between revenue and expenditure in the 20th fiscal year (July 1, 1931 to June 30, 1932).

The largest expenditures are still military expenses and the repayment of principal and interest on debts. To achieve a balance between revenue and expenditure, it is necessary to reduce the burden of the above two items. Currently, the direct military expenditure from the national treasury is approximately 23 million yuan per month. At a time when the communists have not yet been eliminated and the most intense war in our country's history in recent years has just ended, military expenditure cannot be reduced immediately. However, after the suppression of warlords and communists, military expenditure can be gradually reduced. The intention of this department is to gradually reduce military expenditure in accordance with the following plan in order to achieve the goal of reducing annual military expenditure to 21.6 million yuan as resolved by the 日:

July to October of the 20th year: Monthly expenditure of 20 million yuan November of the 20th year to February of the 21st year: Monthly expenditure of 19 million yuan March to June of the 21st year: Monthly expenditure of 18 million yuan

The biggest reason for the budget deficit other than military expenditure is the heavy burden of repaying national debt. Most of the domestic debt raised by the National Government is short-term, of which 360 million yuan (approximately 60% of the total principal) must be repaid in full within three years. This year (20th year), the government must repay approximately 138 million yuan in domestic debt and 3 million pounds in foreign debt (approximately 65 million yuan in national currency), totaling approximately 200 million yuan in national currency. The number of domestic and foreign debts to be repaid in the 21st year is expected to be the same as this year. This number exceeds the deficit of any previous year by far, and the expected deficit in future years is not expected to be as large.

Looking at the budget problem in the future, it seems very bleak at first glance, but it is not impossible to solve if you look closely. Although there are many temporary borrowings, the amount of debt repaid annually is actually greater than the amount of new borrowings, so the national burden is not only not increasing, but is actually decreasing. However, although the total amount of national debt has not increased, the losses from borrowing new to repay old debt interest discounts are very large. The only way to remedy this is to plan comprehensively and discuss it in the long term, raise a large fund to repay the shortest-term debts in advance, and maintain the longer-term debts. If necessary, new public bonds with longer issuance times can be issued based on the total amount of funds raised to attract investment from home and abroad. If this new public bond plan is implemented, the number of debts repaid annually will be reduced, and the budget can be gradually adjusted. Moreover, there will be surplus funds to transfer as collateral for new long-term public bonds for construction purposes. In this way, the government's finances will become more stable, and the credit of various public bonds will be more obvious. The government and bondholders will benefit from each other.

In summary, if it is possible to reasonably limit military expenditure in the future, while issuing long-term public bonds to recover short-term public bonds, and improve all tax revenues, and the political situation is peaceful, the budget deficit problem can be solved. However, the way of governing is not only to focus on balancing revenue and expenditure. Looking closely at our country's financial problems, it is not enough to be satisfied with just balancing the budget. Non-productive expenses should be reduced to the minimum. Balancing revenue and expenditure is the urgent task at hand. However, given the vastness of our country's territory, the annual government expenditure of 50 to 60 million yuan can only cope with the environment. It is impossible to seek construction. Since the foundation of the country was laid and the political power has gradually become unified in the past seven years, the expectations of the people are not limited to 除军阀共匪. The political awareness of the people has risen like the sun rising in the east. Customs autonomy has been achieved, and Likin has been abolished. The country's productivity is no longer restricted. In addition, foreign aggression and the world's economic recession and the tragic fall in silver prices all affect people's lives and promote awareness. What the people look forward to from the government is not just a balanced budget.

Page 11

Continued News

How should the monetary system be improved? How should industry be revitalized? How should industries such as silk and tea be restored to their former glory? How should transportation lines be opened up and popularized? How should education and public health be promoted? This is especially what the people look forward to from the government, and it cannot be evaded with just a balance between revenue and expenditure and a balanced budget.

The government's various departments and agencies, in view of the people's eagerness for construction, have put forward various plans. Many of them are certainly worthwhile, but most of them are just talk because of empty coffers. Each plan also has the sadness of not being coordinated with each other.

When the European War was tense, various countries, in view of the weakness of production efficiency and the disorganization, used government power to summarize, unify, and guide it, and most of them achieved considerable results. In recent years, due to the world's economic recession, the call for rationalization in various countries has been increasing, and the country that has implemented this policy most thoroughly is the Soviet Union. The great program of the Supreme Economic Council's management and control of all national productive forces in the Five-Year Plan will make the Soviet Union a completely industrialized country. Our party is entrusted with the mission of building the country according to the Premier's will, and we should strive to learn from other countries and form a strong and powerful design agency to guide the country's main productive forces to cooperate, set plans, identify goals, and strive forward. We must complete certain planned projects within a certain period of time. Everyone should work together and connect our arms and fingers to implement construction work. Then, just in terms of our country's domestic financial resources, the amount that can be used for this cause is very large.

In short, the government's budget plan should not only be regarded as an annual revenue and expenditure statistics, and it should not be considered self-sufficient to reduce expenditure with a passive policy so that revenue and expenditure can barely be balanced. The people's aspirations are so developed, and the people's morale is so vigorous. After that, the budget should not be bravely promoted in a positive direction to seek surplus power for construction. I have cited the facts and expressed my views respectfully. I hope you will observe and verify them. Minister of Finance Song Ziwen.

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

The case of building a memorial monument to Premier Sun has been determined. The Ximen Yuecheng base was previously requested by the people to be designated as the site for building the memorial monument to Premier Sun by the County Party Department. The County Government decided to collect a small part of the camp site led by private individuals on the base for public use at public expense. Wu, the landlord, filed a lawsuit in the Civil Affairs Department requesting the cancellation of the County Government's disposition. Various organizations once convened a meeting presided over by the County Government to discuss the design drawings and planned to slightly move the memorial monument to the south of the road to show consideration for Wu's houses to avoid demolition. The Construction Bureau drew up the drawings, prepared a budget, and submitted them to the Construction Department for verification. It is now learned that the Construction Department has issued instructions to the county that the relocation of the memorial monument to the south of the road is disrespectful and should be based on the entire planning and construction of the Yuecheng base. The grassy area next to the center is connected by a bay-shaped road, and the houses that should be demolished are indicated clearly in red lines on the original drawing. The Civil Affairs Department also approved the order to the county to comply with the order and rejected Wu's appeal. The case has come to an end. It is now heard that the County Government will convene a land acquisition review meeting in accordance with the order of the department, and the Construction Bureau will also correct the points in accordance with the order of the department and redraw detailed drawings and budgets to be submitted to the department for approval before workers can be recruited for construction.

A fraudster impersonating an official was arrested and brought to Songjiang. Zhang Yishi, a native of Zhuanqiao, is nearly thirty years old and has been a teacher. Recently, he suddenly claimed to be the second director of the Reconnaissance Team of the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department in various townships in Songjiang and Qingpu counties, such as Fengjing, Fanbang, and Xinzhen. He wore a badge with the above title (made of pure gold) and widely recruited reconnaissance team members at a price of 70 yuan, granting them a card with the front printed with the Songjiang-Qingpu County Reconnaissance Certificate and the official seal of the Civil Affairs Department. The reverse side was printed with the words "Second Branch of the Reconnaissance Team of the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department," with the member's name stamp below. He often carried two letters with him, one from Niu Yongjian, the former Minister of Internal Affairs, stating that he was young and capable and could join the Civil Affairs Department. The letter stated that a certain security group had suspected connections with bandits and had been sent to the Civil Affairs Department for verification, signed and sealed. The other was a letter from the First Section of the Fourth Division of the Secretariat of the Provincial Government, with a message from the Chairman inviting him to come to the government to meet and talk on a certain day. Those who were keen on official careers were all shocked. Yang Shijie, an inspector of the Public Security Bureau of the county, discovered the situation and immediately reported to Director Shen that the Civil Affairs Department had not heard of this organization and had not issued any orders. Whether this was impersonating an official or defrauding money, an investigation should be made immediately. Yang was ordered to investigate the school. When he was selling long hair in Jia, he saw that the surname Zhang had been rewritten on the license plate, which was already suspicious, so he interrogated him and searched all the above exhibits one by one, and brought them back to the Public Security Bureau for questioning.

The permission to set up an office across the border has been ordered to be revoked. The Xinzhuang Town Chamber of Commerce has repeatedly requested the National Chamber of Commerce to forward letters to negotiate because the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce set up a branch office in Qibao Town across the border. After failing to obtain results, they submitted a request to the County Government to submit it to the Provincial Government to negotiate with the Municipal Government. It is now learned that the Chamber of Commerce has received instructions from the Provincial Department through the County Government stating that it has approved the Municipal Government's consultation and reply. According to the previous request from the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, the instructions were issued with the approval of the Bureau's original proposal. Before Qibao's administrative takeover, it can temporarily retain its old way of handling matters. In addition to distributing it to the Social Affairs Bureau to order the cancellation, the consultation and review will be conducted. It is heard that the Chamber of Commerce will send personnel to Qibao to take over.

Wuxi

A grocery store in Kaiyuan Township was robbed by thieves. The Jiang Shunji grocery store in Helukou, Kaiyuan Township, was suddenly attacked by more than 20 thieves speaking with northern accents at around 1:00 am yesterday (the 20th). They broke into the house and searched everywhere, taking about half an hour before they looted and whistled away. By the time the 9th branch of the Public Security Bureau learned of the alarm and sent police, the thieves were far away. The total loss of silver, foreign goods, and goods was estimated to be worth more than 500 yuan.

The department ordered a thorough investigation of the tea guest donation. Qian Zhongliang, the head of the first district of Wuxi, previously intended to organize a tea guest donation of one copper coin for each tea in order to raise autonomous funds because the autonomous funds were severely short. Although the restaurants had been notified, it was not implemented because it had not been approved by the superior authorities. However, Wang Debiao and other representatives of tea houses in the city submitted a letter to the Finance Department requesting the cancellation of the original plan. The Finance Department based its presentation on the fact that there was no record of this tea donation. If the presentation was true, it would inevitably be close to harsh levy. Yesterday, a special order was issued to the County Government to investigate and reply.

The murderer in the Qitai Inn case was arrested. Xiang Afu, a cook at the Qitai Inn on Tongyun Road outside Guangfu Gate, was killed after an argument with Gu Ar'er over the collection of a cigarette holder and 15 copper coins. Gu Ar'er was able to escape. It is now learned that after the case occurred, Gu Ar'er was able to escape. It is now learned that after the case occurred, the murderer Gu Ar'er escaped to the Guanyintang in the Cypress Bridge, Tu 583, Jingyun City, outside the East Gate, intending to evade punishment. The incident was discovered by the kitchen owner Xiang Deyu, who personally went to the countryside to trick Ar'er into the city and sent someone to guard him. That night, the head of the township, Meng Yangsu, and the deputy head of the township, Guo Xinliu, believed that Xiang Deyu was also related to the case and intended to settle it privately in the township. However, because the murderer's family was very poor, there was no result. At 4:00 pm yesterday, the family of the deceased decided to report to the County Court for an autopsy. Upon receiving the report, the Prosecutor's Office immediately sent Prosecutor Du, along with the coroner Shen and bailiffs, to the mortuary of the Inn Industry Association for an autopsy. It was found that the deceased Xiang Afu had indeed died from serious injuries. The family of the deceased was instructed to prepare the coffin for burial, and the murderer Gu Ar'er was taken to the court for detention pending the arrival of the related party Xiang Deyu for questioning.

The newspaper delivery industry union was established. The Wuxi newspaper delivery industry union was initiated and organized by Wu Yuanfu, Xu Yongqing, and 26 others. Preparations have been completed, and a general meeting of members was held at 5:00 pm yesterday at the original site of the General Labor Union in Ba'er Lane. The results of the election of committee members were: Wu Yuanfu, Xu Yongqing, Shi Xishan, Sun Xiangfeng, and Zhang Junyun were elected as directors, Wu Renshan and Ding Youren were elected as alternate directors, Wu Zhongming, Xu Yongqing, and Xu Fuyuan were elected as supervisors, and Yin Weiqing was elected as alternate supervisor.

Changzhou

Another kidnapping case occurred near Cuiqiao. Sun Xichang, a resident of Sunjiatang in the 5th district of Wuyi, about five miles away from Cuiqiao Town, has been a chef in Shanghai. Only his wife and a three-year-old child were left at home. The situation was not very wealthy, but the houses they lived in were quite magnificent, which was coveted by bandits. At 1:00 am on the 17th of this month, more than a dozen thieves knocked down the iron door and entered the house, robbing Sun's wife's bedroom and Sun's younger brother Shanchang's house one after another. Unsatisfied with what they had obtained, they kidnapped Sun's three-year-old child and left. Before leaving, they instructed them to prepare 40,000 yuan within three days and send it to 圩　for redemption. At that time, Tian Huo Wang Laosan stepped forward to stop them and was injured by the thieves.

Jiangyin

Regular Convocation of Eight Counties Pacification Conference

The first regiment commander of the Provincial Security Corps stationed in Cheng, and concurrently the commander of the Su-Chang Pacification Sub-district, Zhu County, has scheduled a joint meeting on the 28th of this month at the Guan Yue Temple regimental headquarters on South Street, Jiangyin. The meeting will include all district commanders of land and water military police from Wu County, Wujiang, Kunshan, Qingpu, Changshu, Wuxi, Wujin, and Jiangyin. The command headquarters has prepared proposals and distributed them to the eight counties. Excerpts are as follows:

(1) It has been found that the recent bandit intelligence reports and the actual status tables of armed groups in various counties under the district have often not been submitted on time to the headquarters, making it impossible to clearly understand the recent situation in each county. It is requested that they be submitted by a specified date for assessment.

(2) Any scattered bandits in each county that can be captured and eliminated by the police and militia forces of the county should be strictly searched and arrested by order of the county government within a specified time, and dealt with according to law to eradicate the root cause.

(3) If a large group of bandits suddenly appears in any county, the county government should handle the situation based on the bandit situation, and promptly report the details to the headquarters for verification.

(4) During the pacification period, all armed groups in the district should conduct mutual sentry duties daily. In case of bandit activity, in addition to making every effort to suppress and eliminate them, they should also promptly inform friendly forces to assist in the suppression. If a bandit alert occurs in County A, County B, which is connected, should also be notified for assistance in the suppression, so as to avoid the problem of suppressing them here while they flee there. However, a report must be submitted to the headquarters for record afterward.

(5) During the village cleansing period, private possession of firearms or bandit weapons by civilians should be thoroughly investigated and reported to the headquarters by the county government for submission to the Superintendent's Office for verification.

(6) In areas where traffic is inconvenient and bandits roam, the district office, defense corps, and public security bureau of each county should seriously urge the public to organize civilian sentries to report bandit activity and military liaison matters. If the public in the area fails to comply, they should be punished by military law.

(7) The command headquarters should send a letter to the provincial party headquarters to instruct the party headquarters of each county to organize propaganda teams to promote the benefits of pacification and village cleansing to the public.

(8) If a county or armed group fails to assist when a neighboring area experiences a bandit alert and requests assistance, resulting in an accident, it will be considered as aiding the bandits once verified by the headquarters.

(9) The county where pacification and village cleansing have been completed should report to the headquarters for submission to the Superintendent's Office for record.

(10) All bandits and communists in each county should be thoroughly eliminated within two months.

(11) In counties within this pacification sub-district where there is no bandit disturbance, all armed groups should be instructed to assist the village cleansing bureau in carrying out village cleansing immediately.

(12) During the pacification period, each armed group should report the process of bandit suppression and assistance in village cleansing in detail at any time.

(13) All attending agencies are requested to submit proposals for discussion to ensure thoroughness. Please decide whether this is appropriate.

Past Years' Accumulated Grain Depleted

After the establishment of the Jiangyin Granary Management Committee, it took over the public funds and property management register. Since the implementation of accumulating money instead of grain in Jiangyin, the granary households have stored grain for many years. Upon verification of the original accumulated grain funds, it was found that there was no surplus left in the register. The previous committee was also unable to take over. A total of 104,540 yuan, 2 jiao, 7 fen, and 1 li were found to have been misappropriated. The committee resolved to send the register with the committee's endorsement to the county government for verification and handling.

Election of President and Vice-Presidents of Relief Center

Since the Relief Center was reorganized into a committee system for receiving and organizing, the committee of the center requested the county to officially appoint a president and vice-presidents in accordance with the regulations promulgated by the ministry the other day. County Magistrate Li has now appointed Cao Yuanmo as president, and Zhang Chengshu and Chen Xiaoqing as vice-presidents. Xia Juemou, Zhu Danqing, Qian Hanwu, Gong Yinggeng, Wu Shuying, and Xie Youtao are appointed as fund management committee members and have been reported to the Department of Civil Affairs for record.

Zhenjiang

Peng Yunhui's Malfeasance and Fraud Case

Peng Yunhui, the former captain of the Detective Team of the former Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, was accused by the parties in the Wang kidnapping case in Dongxiang of fraud and dereliction of duty. He was sentenced to three months in prison by the court. Peng appealed to the High Court, which changed the sentence to four years. He appealed again to the Supreme Court, which reduced the sentence to two years. Peng still refused to accept the sentence and filed an extraordinary appeal, which was sent back to the Suzhou High Court for retrial. The sentence was changed to one year and two months, and the complainant was refunded 656 yuan. Peng has been involved in this case for a long time and has stated that he will accept the sentence and wait for execution.

Establishment of the Journalists Association

The Zhenjiang journalists initiated preparations to establish the Journalists Association because the Jiangsu Provincial Party Headquarters recently issued organizational guidelines for the establishment of journalists associations in various counties, which were limited to this month. The preparations have now been completed, and a permit has been issued by the county party headquarters. Therefore, a founding meeting was held at 2:00 PM yesterday in the auditorium of the county party headquarters, and executives were elected. Thirty-seven members attended. Yao Qisu, a representative of the county party headquarters, provided guidance, and Xu Baqun, a representative of the county government, supervised the election. Wang Zhenxian was elected as the temporary chairman by public recommendation. After the ceremony, ballots were cast to elect executives. As a result, Guan Qizi, Tong Xiping, Wang Shaoxian, Tang Zhenqiu, Jiang Xiaochen, Dai Biao, and Dai Jiesan were elected as executives. Jiang Huixing, Zhao Weichuan, and Ma Yinbing were elected as alternate executives.

Yangzhou

Bandits Discovered Near Suining City

The Superintendent's Office of Pacification received a telegram from Suining County on the 18th, stating that bandit leader Wang Yijun led more than 100 bandits to harass the area near Guandi Temple, Wangsu Village, and Sunjia Temple, more than 20 li east of the city. Commander Zhang of the Xu-Hai Pacification Sub-district led the first and second regiments and the direct troops of the division headquarters to encircle and suppress them on the morning of the 17th.

Reorganization of the County Education Association

After the County Education Association ceased its activities, Du Zhaotang was sent by the County Reorganization Committee to take over, and Wu Zunyi, Wan Dingxiang, Tang Shou, Zhao Qi, and Xiang Shucheng were appointed as five instructors to guide the organization of the Education Association. Yesterday (18th), the instructors held their first conversation meeting at the county party headquarters at 2:00 PM and resolved to reorganize into eight districts according to the original administrative divisions. The instructors will be responsible for guiding the organization of the district education associations, which must be established before the 25th. The County Education Association will be formally established before the 31st. Member registration must be completed before the 25th.

Rugao

A Fire Caused a Loss of Nearly a Thousand Gold

Yesterday afternoon, two children were playing with fire in the Zhu Bajun area south of the Longwang Temple in Matang, when a fire suddenly broke out. At that time, the east wind was strong, and the fire spread to the houses. In an instant, eight or nine thatched houses were reduced to ashes. It is reported that the loss was about eight or nine hundred yuan.

Scheduled Collection of Banquet Donations

In order to compensate for education expenses, the Bureau of Education once drafted regulations for the collection of banquet donations in accordance with the methods of Wuxi and Nantong counties and submitted them to the county government for submission to the Department of Finance for verification. Subsequently, the Department of Finance submitted it to the 375th meeting of the provincial government, which decided to approve it. It is now learned that the banquet donations have been decided by the County Bureau of Education and the Bureau of Finance to be contracted out by merchants in districts and will be implemented from April 1st.

Nantong

Provincial Government Protects the Fishing Season Along the Coast of Jiangbei

Due to the rampant pirates along the coast of Jiangbei, the provincial government believed that the fishermen did not dare to go to sea during the current fishing season. Representatives were sent to the province to petition. The representatives have now returned to Nantong. The province has indicated that it will work with the Superintendent of Pacification to protect the fishing season along the coast of Jiangbei. The matter involves military plans and cannot be disclosed.

Difficulty in Increasing Taxes on Enclosed Land Along the River

The Provincial Government Committee decided to increase taxes on enclosed reed fields along the river in Tongyi, following the example of Changshu. Jiang Yongyi was appointed to handle the matter in Nantong. Commissioner Jiang arrived in Nantong and, together with the county government, surveyed the fields. Due to the collapse of the reed fields in the northern part of the enclosed sea sand area, it was not possible to proceed as planned and a report was submitted to the province for verification.

Relief for the Severe Collapse of the Riverbank

The collapse of the riverbank in Tongyi has become increasingly severe recently. The disaster victims along the river have appealed to the province and county for relief. Currently, the urgent task is to build a retreating bank and a healthy retaining wall, which will cost 300,000 yuan. The provincial government has decided that the province and county will each bear half of the cost. The Bank Protection Committee has continued to report to the provincial government, requesting that a special commissioner be sent to Nantong to manage the county funds. The county funds are insufficient, and it is requested that some of the 40% of Zhang Jian's confiscated property be allocated to facilitate progress.

Huzhou

Henan Residents Beat and Injure Villagers

Around 1:00 PM on the 15th of this month, in the Nanyang Dou area of Shanlian Town in the southeast of this city, a group of itinerant residents from Henan, led by Ren Hesan, drove more than 300 yellow ducks into the fields. Farmers such as Pan Shirui were working in the fields and, fearing that the ducks would harm the spring flowers, advised them to stop. Ren held a grudge against Pan and gathered forty or fifty vagrants who were living in the area. Each of them carried hoes, wooden sticks, and other implements and rushed to the village. Without asking any questions, they beat the villagers indiscriminately, injuring many. They also tied up the villagers Pan Yatou and Shen A'duo and beat them severely in the thatched shed where the itinerant residents lived. When the villagers saw this, they reported it to the village chief, who informed the Shanlian Town Defense Corps and requested that they send a team to suppress the violence. Chief Zhang of the corps personally led more than ten militiamen to the thatched shed, rescued the injured Pan and Shen, and took Ren Hesan's brother, Ren Awu, and a worker to the Wu-Xing Local Court for investigation yesterday.

Jinan

Resolution of the Case of a Female Student Injured by a Car

Chen Yuxi, a student at Jinan Provincial Women's Middle School, was injured by a military vehicle No. 6 while lining up to attend a meeting on the anniversary of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's death. Because the car owner firmly refused to admit responsibility, the education community launched a public appeal to the party and government authorities, making six demands. After Director of Education He Siyuan returned to Jinan on the 16th, the car owner admitted to injuring the student, and the matter is expected to be resolved peacefully. The student has been discharged from the hospital and returned home, but she is still mentally distraught.

(1) Oath of the Chinese Boy Scouts

I, [Name], swear to abide by Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings, firmly adhere to the rules of the Chinese Boy Scouts, and devote myself to the following three things throughout my life:

First, to practice the teachings of loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, faith, righteousness, peace, and to be a loyal citizen of the Republic of China;

The blue sky is high, the white sun is bright!

Chairman Chiang's Remarks on the Change of Presidents at Tsinghua University

(Central News Agency)

The change of presidents at Tsinghua University has attracted much attention. Yesterday, Chairman Chiang made the following remarks to a reporter about the approval of the resignation of former President Luo Jialun. The record is as follows:

President Luo has achieved remarkable results in running Tsinghua University. Not only has the university's affairs improved day by day, but everything has been done in accordance with the principles of our party and the policies of the central government. He has made great efforts to rectify the academic atmosphere and unify thought. When the reactionary forces of Feng Yuxiang were rampant, President Luo worked hard in the north to uphold justice and to make students understand right and wrong and the location of obedience. This was particularly appreciated by the central government. Therefore, although Luo repeatedly requested to resign since last year, the government earnestly persuaded him to stay. During the spring, I personally urged him to return to the university to preside over it in Hankou twice. Later, the central government decided to appoint him as the director of academic affairs of the Central Political School. The Central Political School is very important to the party and the country. All comrades in the central government believe that it is essential to have someone as loyal, hardworking, knowledgeable, and experienced as Comrade Luo to take on the role. In fact, it was difficult to balance both roles. Therefore, his resignation was finally approved at the State Council meeting and Wu Nanxuan was appointed instead. President Wu is loyal and sincere, and the affairs of Tsinghua University will surely develop along the right track. The report in the newspaper yesterday that I met with students on Tuesday and that the conversation did not match the situation at the time is inaccurate. The government can consider the wishes of the students if they are reasonable, but the government will naturally make the final decision on the selection and appointment of personnel.

Measures for Rewarding Works on Party Ideology

Passed by the 132nd Central Standing Committee

(Central News Agency)

The text of the measures for rewarding works on party ideology, as passed by the Central Standing Committee today (19th), is as follows:

1. These measures are specifically formulated to reward works on party ideology in order to promote the party's ideology, policies, and to clarify historical facts.

2. A Review Committee on Party Ideology Works shall be established to assess the value and scope of works on party ideology. The organization of the committee shall be determined separately.

3. All lengthy works on party ideology, whether published or unpublished, may be submitted to the Review Committee for review.

4. Works on party ideology shall include the following categories:

(1) Works elucidating the party's ideology;

(2) Works elucidating the party's policies;

(3) Works elucidating the party's historical facts;

(4) Translations that elucidating the party's ideology, policies, programs, and historical facts;

(5) Literary and social science works related to the party's ideology, policies, programs, and historical facts.

5. Works that meet one or more of the following criteria shall be eligible for awards from the Central Government:

(1) Those that make a special contribution to the party's ideology, policies, and historical facts;

(2) Those that can portray party ideology as excellent literary works;

(3) Those that provide a systematic explanation of the party's ideology and policies;

(4) Those that provide a precise critique of reactionary works based on the party's ideology, policies, and historical facts.

6. The methods of awarding may be one or more of the following:

(1) Awarding a certificate of merit;

(2) Recommending for publication;

(3) Issuing a directive to the whole country to use as reference materials for the party ideology courses in schools or as compulsory reading for party members;

(4) Awarding a bonus, with the amount divided into five grades: Grade A: 2,000 yuan; Grade B: 1,000 yuan; Grade C: 500 yuan; Grade D: 300 yuan; Grade E: 200 yuan.

The copyright of the rewarded works shall remain with the author even if the bonus has been obtained.

7. If the author of a rewarded work wishes to revise all or part of the work, the revised manuscript must be submitted to the Review Committee for review before it can be published.

8. These measures shall be implemented upon resolution by the Central Executive Committee.

Organizational Regulations and Outline of Action Plan for the Central Film Culture Propaganda Committee

||Passed by the 132nd Meeting of the Central Standing Committee||

(Central News Agency)

The text of the Organizational Regulations and Outline of Action Plan for the Central Film Culture Propaganda Committee, as passed by the Central Standing Committee today (19th), is as follows:

(A) Organizational Regulations

Article 1. This committee shall be responsible for all matters related to film culture propaganda throughout the country under the command of the Central Executive Committee.

Article 2. The committee shall consist of seven to nine members. In addition to the Minister of Propaganda, Minister of Education, and Minister of Interior of the Central Government being ex officio members, the remaining members shall be appointed by the Central Executive Committee from persons with rich film knowledge and experience.

Article 3. The committee shall elect three standing committee members from among themselves to handle daily affairs.

Article 4. The organization of the committee is as follows: (omitted)

(If shooting sound films, a dubbing group can be added)

Article 5. Each department shall have a director, and the film personnel training institute shall have a director. All shall be appointed by the Central Executive Committee upon request from the committee.

Article 6. Each section under each department shall have a chief executive officer to be responsible for handling the affairs of the section.

Article 7. Each section may have a number of staff and recorders depending on the complexity of the affairs.

Article 8. All chief executives and staff below the chief executive officer of each department of the committee shall be appointed by the committee upon the recommendation of the director of the department.

Article 9. The organizational regulations of the film personnel training institute shall be determined separately.

Article 10. The committee shall hold a committee meeting once every two weeks.

Article 11. The detailed rules of procedure for each department and the training institute of the committee shall be determined separately.

Article 12. These regulations shall be implemented upon resolution by the Central Executive Committee.

Outline of Action Plan

1. Based on all the teachings of Dr. Sun Yat-sen and the current administrative orders of the central government, determine all the principles for film production.

2. After the formal establishment of the committee, the General Affairs Department, the Editorial Department, the Photography Section of the Production Department, and the Film Personnel Training Institute should be established immediately.

3. The start-up cost is a total of 40,000 yuan in national currency (including the start-up cost of the training institute). The monthly recurring expenses should not exceed 8,000 yuan at most.

4. After the formal establishment of the committee, it should engage in the creation of scripts and the training of staff. This editing and training will be a six-month period.

5. If the funds are abundant after six months, preparations should be made to build a photography studio and a film production plant. The start-up cost is about 150,000 to 300,000 yuan, and it should be completed within four months. A national film theater, photography studio, and film production plant should be established, and all positions should be filled by students graduating from the actor training institute.

6. If funding is difficult after six months, the completed scripts will be entrusted to a suitable film company for production. The committee will send directors and other key staff to manage the matter. The students of the training institute will be introduced by the committee to various film companies for service or reorganized into a Central Art Propaganda Troupe to carry film projectors and other entertainment items to various places for touring propaganda.

7. Matters related to overseas propaganda shall be handled by the committee by requesting the diplomatic officials stationed in each country to select suitable personnel to take on the task.

8. All expenses of the committee shall be raised by the Central Government.

The Origin of the Creation

The Central Film Culture Propaganda Committee was proposed by Mr. Li Yiyuan, Dai Ce, and Wang Shilian, graduates of the National Conservatory of Arts and Crafts in Paris, France. The proposal was submitted by Central Committee members Wu Zhihui and Chu Minyi and passed by the Central Political Conference. The origin of the creation is recorded as follows:

It is believed that the film industry has developed rapidly in recent years, and all countries attach great importance to it. This is indeed the most effective tool for propaganda for various undertakings, and its effect is far above written language. Although China's film industry is still young, and there are one or two privately run enterprises, they are very simple. It is considered that in this era of political tutelage, with the beginning of construction, and with the abandonment of various undertakings, if it is desired to promote various undertakings, there must first be considerable propaganda, then film is still necessary. Therefore, it is proposed that the Central Government organize the Central Film Culture Propaganda Committee to facilitate propaganda. The more prominent of its effects are described as follows:

1. Propagandizing the Principle of People's Livelihood. Dr. Sun Yat-sen devoted himself to the revolutionary cause for forty years. The purpose of this was to seek freedom and equality for China. Only when the people have first settled down and are able to live in peace can they reach the realm of freedom and equality. Therefore, Dr. Sun Yat-sen's unique vision places primary importance on the people's livelihood. Unfortunately, the strength of propaganda was not widespread, and as a result, it failed to become popularized. In recent years, the country has faced many difficulties, and the people's livelihood has become increasingly difficult. The unemployed have either entered the military or become bandits to maintain their lives, causing disasters to the country and disrupting the good people. Even those who have businesses are unable to live in peace, placing the country in a dangerous situation. The reason for this is that the Principle of People's Livelihood is not being discussed. Therefore, the fundamental solution is to make every effort to propagandize the Principle of People's Livelihood on the one hand, and to instruct the people on how to implement the Principle of People's Livelihood in terms of food, clothing, housing, and transportation so that the people can have happiness. It is hoped that theory and practice will be equally emphasized to make it easier to promote. However, the scientific knowledge of the Chinese people is shallow, and dialects vary from place to place. If we rely on written propaganda, we are afraid that it will not be popular, so that 95% of the people who are illiterate will be able to understand it. If we rely on lectures, there will be the disadvantage of linguistic barriers. So, what can be done? Only artistic and scientific film propaganda can make the deepest impression on the people, with easy, fast, broad and宏 effects, so that the unemployed vagrants all know the joy of earning a living, and the good people with businesses live in peace and enjoy their work. This can achieve the effect of潜移默化 in the invisible.

The Second Finals of the Vanguards Basketball Tournament between China and the United States

7:30 PM Tonight:: If China Wins:: There is Hope for the Championship || Korea vs. Jewish:: Competing for the Losing Championship Tonight ||

Taxpaying Chinese Association Re-election Voting Yesterday Morning

Ballots Counted Today; The Shanghai Public Concession Taxpaying Chinese Association held its tenth election and began voting at 9:00 AM yesterday. The situation is recorded as follows:

Attendees; Ye Mujiu from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Shanghai Office; Shanghai Mayor Zhang Yueche; Wang Xiaolai; Xu Jili; Fang Jiaobo; Lin Kanghou; Hu Fengxiang; Yuan Jinchu; Lao Jingxiu; Qian Xinzhi; Qian Longzhang; Yan Junan; Wu Yunzhai; Chen Zheqing; Ye Fuxiao; Wu Jingxiong; Xu Xinliu; Yu Qiaqing; Qian Chengxu; Wu Zhihao; and dozens of others.

Meeting Agenda; (1) Bow three times to the Party Flag, National Flag, and Sun Yat-sen's portrait; (2) Read Sun Yat-sen's will; (3) Chairman Wang Xiaolai reports on the preparations for the re-election; (4) Appoint ballot supervisors: Hu Fengxiang, Cheng Xiechun, Fang Jiaobo, and Zhang Yichen are recommended as ballot supervisors; (5) Inspect and seal the ballot boxes, verifying that they are sealed and that Ye Hongji (Mujiu), the representative of the Foreign Affairs Office, signs his name on the seams to show solemnity, and hands the keys to Representative Ye for safekeeping; (6) Begin voting.

Voting Situation; Many people went to vote in person and the traffic was continuous in the morning and afternoon. Some were delivered on foot or sent by mail. The ballot paper of Wang Rutang, Minister of Foreign Affairs, was sent by express mail from Nanjing. The ballot boxes were temporarily sealed at 5:00 PM, and some people still sent ballot papers, which were kept separately and will be put in public this morning.

Taking care of the venue; From 9:00 AM to 5:00 PM, Lin Kanghou, Hu Fengxiang, Tao Leqin, Xu Fansun, Gao Wosheng, and Zhu Baoluo and Zhang Zhiseng from the Citizens' Federation took care of the venue all day. Mayor Zhang Yuejun also visited the meeting at 2:00 PM for a week.

Temporarily Sealing Ballot Boxes; At 5:00 PM, the voting time was temporarily suspended as usual. The ballot boxes were sealed and affixed with seals, and Lin Kanghou and Hu Fengxiang signed the seam markings. The ballot boxes were stored in the basement of the Bank Association Building and sealed for safekeeping.

Today's Schedule; The ballot counting will still be held at the Bank Association Building at No. 4 Hong Kong Road at 9:00 AM today. The agenda for today's meeting is as follows: (1) Bow to the Party Flag and National Flag; (2) Read Sun Yat-sen's will; (3) Elect ballot counters, vote callers, and tally clerks; (4) Open the ballot boxes; (5) Report the number of votes; (6) Report the names of the elected persons.

Municipal Public Bonds Drawn for the First Time Yesterday

Total of $210,000 in winning bonds; Payment of cash from the 31st of this month; Last year, the municipal government issued $3 million in municipal public bonds. The Municipal Finance Bureau held the first drawing yesterday in the deliberation hall of the Bank Association, presided over by Director Tang Naikang, with Xu Youru recording and registering, and Chen Kecheng as the emcee announcing the numbers. The details are recorded below:

Representatives from Various Parties Present; Representatives included Wang Shiduo from the Supervisory Yuan; Pang Zeen from the Ministry of Finance; Mayor Zhang, Zhu Hao, Zhu Ming, Yuan Shengting, and Chen Kecheng from the Municipal Government; Dai Hongji from the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court; Wu Deying from the Local Court; Zhu Jianming from the Bank of China; Li Tisheng from the Central Bank; Jin Jingyuan and Shen Zhonghao from the Bank of Communications; Xia Peide from the Municipal Bank; Xu Jili from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce; Tao Leqin from the Fund Management Committee; Lin Kanghou from the Bank Association; Yan Junan from the Money Industry Association; and Yu Qiaqing, Fang Jiaobo, Fan Jietang, and more than a hundred others.

Various Supervisors; The supervisors were Wu Deying, Wang Shiduo, Jin Jingyuan, Yan Junan, Tao Leqin, Li Tisheng, Zhu Jianming, Xia Peide, Fan Jietang, Pang Zeen, and ten others.

Meeting Agenda; (1) Ring the bell to start the meeting; (2) Pay the highest respects to Sun Yat-sen's portrait; (3) Read the will; (4) Silence; (5) Mayor's speech; (6) Chairman's report; (7) Invite supervisors to check the signed checks and check stubs; (8) Perform the lottery; (9) Tea and refreshments; (10) Adjournment

Mayor's Speech Excerpt; Today is the first drawing of municipal public bonds. I am honored to have all the representatives present to participate in the supervision. Since the establishment of the Shanghai Municipal Government in the 17th year of the Republic of China, it has been actively carrying out various new construction projects in order to create a new Shanghai. Since I took office, I have been thinking about further advancing the municipal construction. However, construction projects require funds everywhere, which has made the municipal government's expenses feel even more enormous. Therefore, there is the issuance of public bonds. The issuance of public bonds does not have any difficulties in fact, because on the one hand, it can get the enthusiastic support of all sectors, and on the other hand, it is for the public interest of the citizens. However, the municipal government has specially formed a public bond fund management committee to show its creditworthiness, and the members of the committee are all leaders and prestigious figures from all sectors. Therefore, in terms of credit, not only I dare to be responsible, but also the fellow citizens and the members of the fund management committee dare to be responsible. As for the use of these 3 million public bonds, 1 million will be used to establish a municipal bank, 500,000 will be used to construct the central area of the city, 200,000 will be used to reorganize old public bonds, and the rest will be used for new construction projects other than the main roads of the city. The future new construction of Shanghai will also start from here. Moreover, the refunding fund for this drawing not only does not feel insufficient, but also has a surplus, which further shows the municipal government's prudence regarding public bonds. After the speech, Chairman Tang Naikang, Director of the Bureau, reported on the situation in a similar way.

Lottery Results; A total of seven bonds were drawn this time, each worth $30,000, for a total amount of $210,000. The winning numbers are 12, 46, 60, 63, 74, 85, 98. All winning bonds will be paid in cash, including principal and interest, from the Shanghai Central, Communications, China, and Municipal Banks starting from the 31st of this month.
